Certainly! Now that Property 6 has been selected, let's explore the joint financing solutions and mortgage options typically available for a CAD $460,000 property in Toronto.

Based on standard offerings, here's a general overview:

**1. Common Mortgage Terms:**
*   **Fixed-Rate Mortgages (e.g., 5-year fixed):** These offer stability with a locked-in interest rate for a set period, typically 3 or 5 years. This means your payments remain consistent, providing predictability.
*   **Variable-Rate Mortgages:** These have interest rates that fluctuate with the market prime rate. While they can offer lower initial payments, they come with the risk of increasing payments if rates rise. Terms often range from 3 to 5 years before renewal.

**2. Estimated Interest Rates:**
While rates can change daily, for a property in this range and considering joint applicants, you could generally expect:
*   **Fixed-Rate:** Currently, estimated fixed rates might hover around **5.5% - 6.5%** for a 5-year term, depending on lender and applicant profile.
*   **Variable-Rate:** Estimated variable rates might start slightly lower, perhaps around **5.8% - 6.8%**, but are subject to market changes.

**3. Down Payment Requirements:**
As previously mentioned, a **20% down payment (CAD $92,000)** is typical for a traditional mortgage to avoid mortgage default insurance premiums. However, for first-time buyers, options like a 10% down payment (CAD $46,000) might be available, though this generally incurs additional insurance costs.

**4. Other Significant Terms for Joint Applicants:**
*   **Credit Scores:** Lenders will assess the credit scores of both applicants. Strong scores for both can lead to better interest rates and terms.
*   **Income Verification:** Both your and Alex's income will be verified to determine affordability and borrowing capacity.
*   **Debt-to-Income Ratio:** Lenders will look at the combined debt of both applicants relative to their combined income.
*   **Legal & Arrangement Fees:** As indicated, an arrangement fee (e.g., CAD $1200 for a traditional mortgage or CAD $800 for first-time buyers) will apply. You'll also need to budget for legal services (e.g., Basic Legal Package at CAD $800) and potentially a property survey.

To get a precise quote tailored to your specific financial situation as joint applicants, we would recommend a formal mortgage pre-approval application with a lender. This would give you a clear understanding of your exact borrowing power and the best rates available to you.
</output_to_ai_assistant>
